\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ A\ dial\ jpeg\ file\ can\ be\ converted\ to\ a\ byte\ array\ using:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ https://tomeko.net/online\_tools/file\_to\_hex.php?lang=en}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Paste\ the\ byte\ array\ into\ a\ sketch\ tab\ "{}jpeg\_name"{}\ and\ add}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ two\ lines\ at\ the\ start\ with\ a\ unique\ array\ name:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ const\ uint8\_t\ \ jpeg\_name[]\ PROGMEM\ =\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ At\ the\ end\ add:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \};}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ See\ example\ below.\ Include\ the\ tab\ in\ the\ main\ sketch,\ e.g.:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#include\ "{}jpeg\_name.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
